DIALOG_MSG_VO_HELP = "{33FF33}Short description about the vehicle objects..", "Ok"
You have a change to attach 60 objects to your vehicle!\n
You can create and attach objects with the /aotv command. If you are satisfied with the object you can save it too.
To save it use the /svo command, to load it use the /lvo command.
If you want to save an object set (all of the objects on the vehicle) then type /svoset and /lvoset to load it.
But all of the objects have to be saved (with /svo), or you can't save your voset with the /svoset!\n
Parancsok:

{" #XCOLOR_GREEN "} {" #XCOLOR_YELLOW "}/svo - Save object on the vehicle in the entered slot.
{" #XCOLOR_GREEN "} {" #XCOLOR_YELLOW "}/fsvo - With this you can overwrite your object.
{" #XCOLOR_GREEN "} {" #XCOLOR_YELLOW "}/lvo - Load your saved object into the entered slot.
{" #XCOLOR_GREEN "} {" #XCOLOR_YELLOW "}/voname - Renaming the saved object.
{" #XCOLOR_GREEN "} {" #XCOLOR_YELLOW "}/svoset - Saving all of the objects and create an object set.
{" #XCOLOR_GREEN "} {" #XCOLOR_YELLOW "}/fsvoset - With this you can overwrite your object set(voset).
{" #XCOLOR_GREEN "} {" #XCOLOR_YELLOW "}/lvoset - Load your saved voset.
{" #XCOLOR_GREEN "} {" #XCOLOR_YELLOW "}/vosetname - Renaming the saved voset.
{" #XCOLOR_GREEN "} {" #XCOLOR_YELLOW "}/volist - List of saved objects.

 /login - Log in.
 /stats - User's Statistics. ( If you write an ID behind this, you can watch the player's stats with that ID. )
 /changepass - Changes your password.
 /changename - Changes your name.
 /jailtime - Remaining time in jail.
 /logout - Logs out. (Don't use!)
 /forumregister - Registers to the forum InGame, and attaches your forum account at the same time.
 /myforumacc - Attaches an exist account to the forum.
 /forumstats - Watches forum statistics InGame.
 /styles - Changes fighting style.
 /laser(on/off/col) - Turns the laser on/off, or change its color.
 /readcmds - Reads commands.
 /fly - Turns on/off the fly with the "C" button.
 /allowtime - Sets the time mode to real or InGame.
 /togglevel - Turns on/off saving speed with /s command.
 /fastrespawn - Turns on/off fast respawn after death.
 /mytime - Sets or saves your time.
 /resettime - Deletes saved time.
 /myweather - Sets or saves your weather.
 /resetweather - Deletes saved weather.
 /spawnplace - Changes your spawning place.
 /colors ( /színek ) - Sets your color.
 /savecolor - Saves your current color.
 /rcolor - Sets your color randomly.
 /chatcolor - Changes your chatbox message's color.
 /removechatcolor - Deletes your chat color (sets to white).
 /idcolor - Changes your ID after your name on the chatbox.
 /removeidcolor - Deletes your ID color, so your ID's color will the same as your color.
 /walkstyle - Sets your walking style.
 /findplayer - Search players by their name.
 /findregid - Search players by their RegID.
 /nos - Sets nitrous' style.
 /favwheel - Sets your favorite wheel.
 /leavehq - Leave from your current HQ.×
